		<script type="text/javascript">
							var useragent = navigator.userAgent;
							var navigatorname;
							if (useragent.indexOf('MSIE')!= -1)
							{
							navigatorname="MSIE";
							}
							else if (useragent.indexOf('Gecko')!= -1)
							{
							if (useragent.indexOf('Chrome')!= -1)
							navigatorname="Google Chrome";
							else
							navigatorname="Mozilla";
							}
							else if (useragent.indexOf('Mozilla')!= -1)
							{
							navigatorname="old Netscape or Mozilla";
							}
							else if (useragent.indexOf('Opera')!= -1)
							{
							navigatorname="Opera";
							}
							
							function symbol(code1,code2)
							{
							if (navigatorname == 'MSIE')
								document.write(code1);
							else
								document.write(code2);
							}
							</script>

	<body xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><div class="basic"><p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.1.1 Welcome to Module 2</p>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 27" height="267" width="307" src="module 2_files/image1.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Hi, everyone, and welcome.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'm Andrew, your instructor for week 2 of the Introduction to HTML and CSS course.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this module, we're going to cover global and non global attributes and how to use them, paying close attention to the commonly used ones such as 'id' and 'class'.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In addition, you'll learn about the importance of separating content and style in HTML5, as well as look at the difference between semantic and style tags.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We'll study semantic elements, why they're important, as well as look at their usage in various examples.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, in the second half, we'll cover how to add images to your HTML, and I think you'll agree, images make everything more interesting.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We'll learn how to use the image tag and its attributes, and we would also look at scenarios where it's more appropriate to add images using CSS instead.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Finally, we'll learn how to add hyperlinks to your Web page and their different uses.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>At the end of each subsection, you'll be able to do exercises based on what you've learned and test your knowledge by doing a quiz.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We hope you enjoy the course, and happy learning!</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.1.2 Meaningful Web Pages</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Tags and elements are building blocks of HTML5. However, they can be made so much more exciting with attributes. Let's take a simple element like list. You know how to add one to your page but can you change the order of your list? Or change it<span>
						</span></span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">to an alphabetically ordered list instead of a numerical list? Can you display your list in reverse order? Yes, you can do all this and more using attributes.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Apart from exploring attributes for elements, we will continue to add life to our Web page by adding images and hyperlinks and learning about how to use and place them properly in your Web page.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">In this module, we will also look at creating meaningful Web pages. Imagine you are the Web page designer of an online magazine. You want to have a central article, some aside commentary, captions, a summary of your article, addresses and citations. You also want to provide more detailed information such as, 'This sentence is really important and you need to convey that to the reader'.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">If we just use </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt; </span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">tags and header tags, </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "> to </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h6&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">, visually it might look like what you want, but only a human will be able to read and understand the page. To a browser, there is very little information except that there is text and headings in your page. How can a search engine know what is important? Does a visually impaired person have to listen to the entire page or can they just jump to the article?</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">It is very important to style your Web pages for search engine optimization (SEO) to improve your search engine rankings, and for visually impaired people who access your Web page using assistive technology like screen readers. Semantic markup enables all of this and more.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.1.3 Module 2 - Content</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">2.1 Introduction: </span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Check out this video explaining what you'll be learning about in Module 2 - and wrap your mind around the concept of "semantic markup".</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">2.2 Attributes: </span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Here you will build on to what you have already learned about attributes.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">2.3 Semantic meaning: </span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Explaining the difference between 'semantic' and 'style'.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">2.4 Images: </span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Learn how, when, and where to best utilize images in your Web pages.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">2.5 Hyperlinks: </span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">They are the connections that allow the world to jump from place to place on the Web. Explore the secrets of this powerful mechanism!</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.2.1 Introduction</p>
			<div>
				<p>We learned a little bit about what attributes are in the previous module. Let's look into it in more depth, by using examples.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here is an ordered list:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l1 style_l1 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">  &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Lights</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l2 style_l2 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">  &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Camera</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l3 style_l3 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">  &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Action</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l4 style_l4 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Output:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>1.<span>
					</span>Lights</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>2.<span>
					</span>Camera</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>3.<span>
					</span>Action</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If i want an ordered list to start with the number 5 instead of 1 (as it does by default), let's code like this:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;ol</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">start</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"5"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l1 style_l1 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">  &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Lights</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l2 style_l2 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">  &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Camera</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l3 style_l3 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">  &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Action</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l4 style_l4 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Output:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="background-color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">5. Lights</span><br/><span style="background-color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">6. Camera</span><br/><span style="background-color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">7. Action</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here, using the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">start</span> attribute, we made our list start with 5 instead of 1.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Like <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">start</span>, we have many useful attributes we will see in this section that can affect your element. Attributes are a significant part of HTML. Tags and attributes make up the language. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Syntax:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Attributes are used in tags to further define the tag:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>It is used inside the opening tag it is applied to and should be added after a space from the tag name: <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;ol start="5"&gt;</span>. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">start</span> attribute is used inside the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span> tag. </p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; ">start="5"</span><br/>Attribute name, equal sign, opening quote, attribute value, closing quote</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Attributes are a name-value pair: <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; ">start="5"</span><br/>name: start<br/>value: any positive integer</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The only exception to the name-value pair is if the attribute is a 'boolean attribute'. These attributes have only two types of values - true or false. But instead of writing "true" or "false" for its value, you add the attribute name to indicate true and omit it to indicate false. An example is the 'reversed' attribute in an ordered list <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span>. Adding this attribute is an indication that the list order should be reversed (in descending order). <br/><span style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">    </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; "> &lt;ol reversed&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>A tag can have multiple attributes:<br/><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; ">   &lt;ol start="5"&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;</span><span style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "><br/></span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; ">   &lt;ol id="cinema" class="attribute-list" start="5"&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;</span><span style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "><br/></span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; ">   &lt;ol start="5" class="attribute-list"&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Example #1: the 'id' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>Imagine you have two paragraphs in your HTML page:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">I am paragraph 1 and I want to be in red</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l1 style_l1 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">I am paragraph 2 and I want to be in blue</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; ">Your task is to make the text color of the first paragraph </span>red<span style="font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; "> and the other </span>blue<span style="font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; ">. How do we do that? </span>You add styling to your HTML document through CSS. CSS is a style sheet language where you add any presentation related information for your HTML document. You will learn about this in the next chapter. In this case, you will have to write code in your style sheet to inform that it needs to change the text colors respectively. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But to identify each paragraph, we need to give them each a name first so we can instruct our style sheet to make X red and Y blue. This unique<span style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "><span><span></span>
						</span>name we give each element is called an 'ID'. This is very similar to your school or corporate ID that is unique to you. No one else in your company will have the same ID as you. </span><span style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:13.5pt; ">id</span><span style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> is an attribute. It should be unique to the element; we know how more than one people having the same ID can just cause a lot of confusion. </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"para1"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">I am paragraph 1 and I want to be in red</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l1 style_l1 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"para2"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">I am paragraph 2 and I want to be in blue</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here, we can style <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; ">para1</span> and <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; ">para2</span> separately using CSS. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute helps us do this by letting us give each paragraph an ID.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Example #2: the 'class' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>A similar attribute is <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span>. <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> like <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> is a very useful attribute and one you will be using very frequently. Let's assume you are an author of a book. You like<span>
					</span>poems and you want to include at least 20 of them in your new book. You add IDs for them: 'poem1', 'poem2', 'poem3'.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You want your poems to look different from your other text. Grey text color, italic and bold. Like this:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; ">To move, to breathe, to fly, to float,</span><span style="font-size:11.5pt; font-family:Verdana; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Verdana; font-size:11.5pt; "><br/></span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; ">To gain all while you give,</span><span style="font-size:11.5pt; font-family:Verdana; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Verdana; font-size:11.5pt; "><br/></span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; ">To roam the roads of lands remote,</span><span style="font-size:11.5pt; font-family:Verdana; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Verdana; font-size:11.5pt; "><br/></span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; ">To travel is to live.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; ">- Hans Christian Andersen</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>All poems have the same requirements.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you use the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute, you can instruct the stylesheet to style each poem in a particular way. It will look something like (we will learn how to write proper styles in the next chapter, so for now we will just phrase it in English) -</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>'Make poem1's text color grey, italic and bold'<br/>'Make poem2's text color grey, italic and bold'<br/>'Make poem3's text color grey, italic and bold'</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Can you imagine how repetitive your style sheet will look if you have to instruct it to do the same thing 20 times for different poem IDs? HTML makes it easier. We use the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> attribute. Let's name this class of poems 'poetry'. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"poem1"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"poetry"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">To move, to breathe, to fly, to float...&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l1 style_l1 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"poem2"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">"poetry"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">Roses are red, violets are blue...</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Consolas; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So now, all you have to do in your style sheet, is to instruct it to make all elements belonging to the 'poetry' class grey, italic and bold. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.2.2 Global and Non-Global Attributes</p>
			<div>
				<p>You have seen a few examples of attributes now: <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">start</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span>. All HTML elements have attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>There are two kind of attributes:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:96px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Courier New; padding-right:20px;">o</span>Global</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:96px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Courier New; padding-right:20px;">o</span>Non-global</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Global attributes</p>
			<div>
				<p>Global attributes can be applied to <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">all tags</span>. They are common attributes. Examples of global attributes are <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id </span>and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span>. There are many more global attributes. Here is a <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Global_attributes#list_of_global_attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDXC4GE5RDZSA3ELTG2V0WKFYV2BOYKXJGAWBO4JEZWG4P3MVEUXZB">list of all the global attributes</span></span></a> and the values they accept.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So attributes like <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id </span>and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class </span>can be applied to any HTML tag.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_HTMLPreformatted style_HTMLPreformatted " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;p id="para1" class="poetry" lang="en"&gt;The global attribute lang takes language codes for values. The code for English is 'en'.&lt;/p&gt;<br/><br/>&lt;html lang="fr"&gt;&lt;/html&gt; - The language attribute tells the browser that the contents of this document will be in french.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_HTMLPreformatted style_HTMLPreformatted " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;ul id="intro-list"&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_HTMLPreformatted style_HTMLPreformatted " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;pre class="html-code"&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Non-global attributes</p>
			<div>
				<p>Non-global attributes<span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span>are attributes applied to a specific instance of a tag. It can be applied to one or more tags. For example, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">start</span> is an attribute for the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span> tag and it cannot be applied on the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt;</span> or <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span> tags, it is specific to only ordered lists <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span>. Another attribute specific to the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span> tag is <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">reversed</span>, which we learned in the last unit as an example of a boolean attribute. The non-global attribute <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">width</span> can be applied to several tags such as <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;input&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;video&gt;</span>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Without</span> the boolean attribute <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">reversed</span>:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">HTML5</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">CSS</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">JavaScript</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">With</span> the boolean attribute <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">reversed</span>:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;ol</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">reversed</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">HTML5</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">CSS</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">JavaScript</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 23" height="281" width="289" src="module 2_files/image2.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">Ordered lists have their own specific attributes and all global attributes can also be applied to them.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">More examples:</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">The image <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img&gt;</span> and hyperlink <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;a&gt;</span> elements, which we will be learning about shortly, have many non-global attributes of their own.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;img&gt;  : </span> src, alt, etc.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;a&gt;</span>  : href, target, download, etc.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">Other than the common global attributes, if you wish to learn about the supported non-global attributes for any element, you can visit the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDL2BL2DACQ1VGK1XJWEYM3NS0JBB3SR0SQKNPIEBLNFJUH4WXOA1P">HTML attribute reference</span></span></a> available at the Mozilla Developer Network (MDN).</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Important: </span>Throughout the course, using the MDN attribute reference, you are encouraged to explore non-global attributes for the elements you learn about or would like to use in your Web pages. In the MDN attribute reference list, you can click on the element's hyperlinked name to be navigated to its page that lists supported attributes for that element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Try this:</span> Navigate to the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID0YZVFUDACYADKFGFMW35M5OU2DMZKB2FMN2YAXO3HX0MDW5Q2CPE">HTML attribute reference</span></span></a> at Mozilla Developer Network and find out which element(s) the attributes <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">muted</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">readonly</span> can be applied to. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Try this:</span> Navigate to the<a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDGXGRHTNXSJHZBV4SHQZ513YKKL552SSSVSZ3IJN2G5X4HRBHJPSF"> HTML attribute reference</span></span></a> at Mozilla Developer Network and find out the non-global attributes that can be applied to the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;li&gt;</span> tag. Search for the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;li&gt;</span> element and then click on it: it will take you to the list tag's page that specifies applicable attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.2.3 Global Attributes: Examples</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Global attribute: 'id'</p>
			<div>
				<p>Like we saw in the previous unit, <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/html5/dom.html#global-attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID0EF1QE3CL4IPJFO511VLVDNSMSGXEH0GTJF4PM5D3V2U3X4DWAH">here is a list of all the global attributes</span></span></a> and the values they accept. To understand attributes, we considered an example of usage <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span>. We are going to look at it in depth here and discuss another global attribute <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute gives your element a unique identifier. In your HTML document, that ID value can only be used in one element. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Naming rules for <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="margin-left:24px; ">Must be of at least one character</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="margin-left:24px; ">Should not contain any spaces</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="margin-left:24px; ">Values are case-sensitive. This means 'QuestioN' and 'question' are NOT the same. That does not mean you can define two different IDs that only differ by case, e.g. "myid" and "MyId". They are different and so legal but it would be extremely confusing to do this!</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"question-about-html"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">How many times can a particular 'id' value be used in an HTML document?</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"html-answer"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Once</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
