				<p><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> is primarily used for:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">1.</span>Styling your element. You can specify the style you want for the element in your style sheet by referencing the 'id'. <br/>Using CSS, you can specify code that will give different styles to "<span style="font-family:inherit; color:#800080; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; ">question-about-html</span>" (e.g.: purple text, center-aligned) and "<span style="font-family:inherit; color:#008000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; ">html-answer" </span> (e.g.: green text)</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">2.</span>Specifying a link target. We will be learning about hyperlinks later in this section. You can link to a section of your HTML page using the 'id' of the section. You should reference the 'id' value with a number sign preceding it - '#id-value'</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:48px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"#introduction"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">1.1 Introduction</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_com style_com " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!-- This is a hyperlink element which we will learn about later in this week --&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:48px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">id</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"introduction"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">This paragraph is the Introduction to the Web page</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">3.</span>In JavaScript, 'id' can be used to manipulate an html element. Using the 'id' of the element, you can write JavaScript code to make it perform an action, i.e. change the text within paragraph tags. </p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Global attribute: 'class'</p>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> attribute, while similar to <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span>, groups a set of elements in the same class. It's name-value pair is <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class="classname"</span>. Unlike <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span>, which is unique to an element,  the same class name can be assigned to more than one element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For example:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"question"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">What is your name?</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"question"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Do you like HTML5?</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Both paragraphs above are grouped under the class named 'question'. An element can have one or more class names. If we also want the second question to be under the 'html' class because it is an HTML related question, you can add two class names by separating them with white space:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"question html"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Do you like HTML5?</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Naming rules for the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> attribute:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Must begin with a letter (a-z or A-Z)</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>First letter can be followed by a letter, digit, hyphen or an underscore</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Values are case-sensitive</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading5 style_Heading5 " style="outline-width:5; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true"><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-size:13.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> is primarily used for:</p>
			<div>
				<p>1. Styling your elements. You can specify the style you want for all the elements that belong to the class in your stylesheet. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"question"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Who are you?</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"answer"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">I am the author</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"question html"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Do you like HTML5?</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"answer"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Yes</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In your CSS, you can include code to style your classes, for example by telling it:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>'question' class: text color is black and text is bold</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>'answer' class: text color is green</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>'html' class: text color is red</p>
			<div>
				<p>The code above will then look like this:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Who are you?</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I am the author</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#EF0000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">Do you like HTML5?</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Yes</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The 'Do you like HTML5?' question has styles for both the 'question' and 'html' classes applied to it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>2. In JavaScript, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> can also be used to manipulate html elements of the same class. </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Global attribute: 'lang'</p>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">lang</span> attribute indicates the language of the text in the element to which it is attached.  Identifying the language of content is increasingly important, as browsers adapt styling and other aspects of the user's experience according to the language of the content. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For example, if you create a page in Japanese, the browser will automatically apply a font that produces Japanese shapes for the characters, rather than Chinese shapes – but only if you have told it that your content is in Japanese. Various presentational aspects also require a knowledge of the language of the content: for example, CSS will style content differently for line-breaking, hyphenation, and text-transforms depending on the declared language. Other features, such as spell-checking and voice browsers for visually-challenged people, also work differently according to which language the content is in.  For more details see <a href="https://www.w3.org/International/questions/qa-lang-why"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDAF1IPWMRRGQGDYN3RWZTN3DQADBGKOOKM5GPUYE2PP51E5KJCBIK">Why use the language attribute?</span></span></a>
				</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The value of a <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">lang</span> attribute must be a language tag that is composed of one or more subtags defined in the <a href="https://www.iana.org/assignments/language-subtag-registry"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDVJE21IM0FKBNNGPJYSNFDLPXRBLJFUZ1TJG13BHYTPZUJXIM5KBH">IANA Language Subtag Registry</span></span></a>. Multiple subtags are separated by hyphens.  (Do <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">not</span> use the ISO lists of languages and countries! Those lists are already subsets of the IANA registry.) You may find it easier to look up subtags using the unofficial <a href="https://r12a.github.io/app-subtags/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDRP1DYCFTPYPXEWZZIM4N3C4EGE1TCH2LASUX2PBSO1VG4WAGL5EO">Language Subtag Lookup</span></span></a> tool.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You should <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">always declare the language of your page in the &lt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Courier New; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Courier New; font-size:13.5pt; ">html&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> tag</span>.  You can also declare the language of content within the page by attaching a <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">lang</span> attribute to an element that contains it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For example:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;html</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">lang</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">"en-GB"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">...</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/html&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;p&gt;In French you'd say &lt;span lang="fr"&gt;On voit souvent des chats sur le Web.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The first example above shows how you can qualify the language (English) with a region subtag (GB) to specify British English.  This distinction can be useful for spellchecking your source. You can also add other subtags, such as scripts and variant labels to further refine the language. However, the golden rule is to always keep the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">lang</span> value as short as possible, and only use additional subtags when you have a good reason (e.g. use just ja for Japanese, not ja-JP). For more information, see the article <a href="https://www.w3.org/International/questions/qa-html-language-declarations"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDYY0OCY25R3YKGZPJM1BHWQ52BC4E0AHHVFX2HZE31Z2THQLU3FRE">Declaring language in HTML</span></span></a>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The second example shows how you could specify a change of language within the document.  This would help a voice browser pronounce the French word 'chats' correctly, meaning 'cats' and not 'chats' in English.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Global attribute: 'title'</p>
			<div>
				<p>Try this: Place your cursor on the word and then on the picture below. Don't click on it, just rest your cursor there. </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading5 style_Heading5 " style="outline-width:5; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:14.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-size:13.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:14.5pt; ">NASA</span></p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 26" height="193" width="193" src="module 2_files/image3.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Did you see the two "secret" messages? A message that appears when you rest your pointer over an element, is called a tooltip. Be it a paragraph, header, image or any element, the title attribute is used to provide additional information about it. It is very useful, to elaborate on abbreviations or add some context. For images, you should use an <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute as there is no guarantee that the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span> attribute will be presented to assistive technology users. The title can be any text value. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;abbr</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:10pt; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">title</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:10pt; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:10pt; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">"National Aeronautics and Space Administration"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">NASA</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10pt; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;/abbr&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.2.4 Global Attributes</p>
			<div>
				<p>References for the video text below:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>
				<a href="https://www.w3.org/2009/cheatsheet/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID2XPL1NYXU1E1EIJD0OTND352JKDDCPMROYMBHVN4IXHFTOUWBZAD">W3C Cheatsheet</span></span></a>
			</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>
				<a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID2NFLU23B5EHYHGC3DRO5GJSI4MWDHDZSTBJTIYEEX4NH3SGWAG1D">Mozilla Developer Newsletter (MDN) Attribute Reference</span></span></a>
			</p>
			<div>
				<p>Hi everyone! Now that we have read a fair amount of information about attributes, we know that there are two kinds, global and non global attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Global attributes apply to all elements be it a paragraph, blockquote, list, image, hyperlink, etc., etc.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And then there are attributes specific to a particular element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Like the start attribute is specific to only ordered lists.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And these are called non global attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But there are so many elements and attributes that it isn't practical to cover them all in this course.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So, we are going to be looking at two good reference Web sites.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The first is the W3C cheatsheet we saw in the pre-work, 'About W3C and the Web’, the section under 'W3C Tools'. This is the cheatsheet.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The second is the Mozilla Developer Network Attribute Reference.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Typically to learn about an element and its attributes, you will visit the HTML5 specification.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This is the HTML5 specification, and under the section global attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But it can be a little overwhelming when you are starting off with HTML5.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The W3C cheatsheet and the MDN attribute reference has this information condensed in a easy to access manner.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I would like to give a little overview on how the W3C cheatsheet works.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can look up any attribute or tag in HTML.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's look at one that we have already learned in week 1, the H1 tag.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>All you have to do is type its name and it’s going to provide the list of attributes that can be applied to this particular tag. The H1 tag only takes global attributes. It doesn't have any non-global attributes of its own.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And it gives a description on what the tag is about and also gives nice tips like use H1 for top level headings or to structure your document.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's also look at the paragraph tag here.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Once again, global attributes can be applied to it. It represents a paragraph.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And what I really like is, you can also navigate directly to the HTML specification, under the paragraph element, and it is going to give you more information and sometimes you can find code samples as well to get a better understanding of the element itself.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, if you'll know more about the list of global attributes, all you have to do is click on this.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And it is going to take you to a list of all the global attributes. Let's look at a few that we have already learned, like the class attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here under elements, it gives you the list of elements that the attribute can be applied to.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Since class is a global attribute, it can obviously be applied to all elements.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And we learned that multiple classes can be applied to all elements if they are split by spaces.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And let's look at one more - the title attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The title attribute is used to provide additional information about something like an abbreviation or add some context to an image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And they give nice little accessibility techniques when it comes to using the title attribute, like provide a title using title element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Not the title attribute and use the title attribute to provide context sensitive help.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And the application of the title attribute varies very slightly depending on the element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Like if you apply it on an abbreviation or a definition, it is used to provide full term or expansion of the abbreviation.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Likewise, it differs slightly for elements like input, link and style.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The best way to use the W3C cheatsheet is, let's say you want to use the blockquote tag.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But you also want to find out the list of attributes that can be applied to it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You go to the blockquote page, and apart from the HTML global attributes, you can also apply one called ‘cite’.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>‘cite’ is used to provide the source of the quotation in the blockquote, mostly for search engines.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You realize you like the cite attribute but you also want to use it in your q tag.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The q tag is used to markup a short quotation.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But does the q tag support the cite attribute?</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Just click on the cite attribute and find out the elements that it can be applied to.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Moving on to the MDN attribute reference list, it works very similar to the W3C cheatsheet.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It gives you a list of all the attributes in the first column.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And then the elements it can applied to, as well as a description on what the attribute does.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's look at our famous 'start' attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The start attribute can be applied to only ordered lists and it defines the first number of the list if it is something other than one.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And if you want to know more information about an element, just click on the element here which will take you to the element's page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And the element's page provides a description of the element itself as well as all the attributes that can be applied to it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you see a little HTML5 label here, it means that this attribute in particular was introduced in HTML5.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And you can also find neat samples illustrating the use of each attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can also find several other HTML elements in the MDN Web site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>They have a nice little navigation on the left that can take you to different element pages.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's it for now and, go ahead and explore attributes and all of the elements you can think of.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.2.5 Activities - Attributes</p>
			<div>
				<p>Please find below suggested activities to help you practice:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; padding-right:20px;">1.</span><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Inter; ">Find the list of supported attributes for the </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;area&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Inter; "> tag. (</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; ">Hint:</span><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Inter; "> use the </span><a href="https://www.w3.org/2009/cheatsheet/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; "><span class="IDP1WAPNQYVWNZHABD2D2SXOF1MEQGWHD1ZEDTG1KROHVKVDDPTRKG">W3C cheatsheet</span></span></a><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Inter; "> or </span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Attributes"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; "><span class="IDBN22H20RC2YRI1NVT4KPWIXSJBVWDBHW35SLMCI4TOEHZVK0024K">MDN attribute reference list</span></span></a><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Inter; ">)</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">2.</span>Create two paragraphs with the same <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> and run your code in a CodePen. What happens? We know the value of the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute must be unique, so why does it behave the way it does? Run your code through the <a href="https://validator.w3.org/#validate_by_input"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; "><span class="IDM0V5H0TXAYX1JQ5E3H1H5P2XIIGQN5OLTSLHF2CM3SYOGB01UB0J">W3C Markup Validator</span></span></a>. Does it throw an error?</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">3.</span>Does an attribute called <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">src</span> exist? What is the purpose of this attribute and what are the elements it can be applied to? (<span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; ">Hint:</span> refer to the W3C HTML5 specification, W3C cheatsheet or MDN attribute reference list)</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">4.</span>Create an ordered list starting with the number 11. Then, reverse the list. Give it the following title (when you hover your mouse, it should display the title as a tooltip): 'Activity List'.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.3.1 Separating Content and Style</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">When writing in hypertext language, it is important to separate content and style. Style should be kept tucked away in Cascading Style Sheets (CSS).</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Let's look at a few interesting tags that lived as exception to this rule and were eventually corrected in HTML5.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span>This text is in <span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;i&gt;</span>Italics<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/i&gt;</span>. It uses the i tag<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span>This text is also in <span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;em&gt;</span>Italics<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/em&gt;</span>. But it uses the em tag!<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span>This text is in <span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;b&gt;</span>Bold<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/b&gt;</span>. It uses the b tag<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span>This text is also in <span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span>Bold<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/strong&gt;</span>. But it uses the strong tag!<span style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">This is how the above HTML code will look in a browser: </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 28" height="281" width="403" src="module 2_files/image4.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It seems redundant for two tags to do the same thing in HTML. While <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;b&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;i&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span> seem no different in a regular Web browser there is an important difference between them.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Semantic vs Style tags</p>
			<div>
				<p>The four tags we saw above can be categorized into style and semantic tags.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Style tags</span>, in HTML4, focused purely on presentation and design. It only talked about how the text should look like on the screen. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Semantic refers to the meaning of words in a language. <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Semantic tags</span> said something about the semantic of the tag. It offered meaning. </p>
			</div>
			<table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:17.08cm; align:center; margin-left:-.132cm; margin-bottom:0cm">
				<tr style="margin:0;border:0;padding:0;visibility:hidden;">
					<th style="width:114.667px;"/>
					<th style="width:124.133px;"/>
					<th style="width:406.733px;"/>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:.732cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Tag</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Type</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Description</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:.75cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;b&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Style</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Makes text bold</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:.732cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;i&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Style</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Makes text italics</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.57cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;em&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Semantic</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Emphasizes text<br/><br/>Text is italics by default in a browser</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.586cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;strong&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Semantic</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Important text<br/><br/>Text is bold by default in a browser</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
			</table>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">&lt;b&gt; vs &lt;strong&gt;</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF0000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">Bold</span><span style="color:#FF0000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "> </span>is a style that makes letters thicker so it stands out among other text but it has no semantic meaning, for example for voice browsers, screen readers, and other types of ways to access the Web. A device like <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amazon_Kindle#Kindle_Paperwhite_.281st_generation.29"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDBPXH5KLY0EISJNBBFSSIXRKBPDIAOOVYPIZLKPXETYTPPOJNOHI">Kindle Paperwhite</span></span></a> that renders text differently, might not pick up the bold.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF0000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">Strong</span><span style="color:#FF0000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "> </span>is an indication of how something should be. It looks like bold in a browser, but it could mean ‘speak with urgency or seriousness’ when reading text aloud. It is semantic in the sense, that we instruct it to be stronger than the text it surrounds which is different from giving instructions on how the text should look in the case of <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;b&gt;</span>. It represents importance, seriousness, or urgency for its contents.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">As a junior developer, you </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">must</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/strong&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> submit your work for code review!</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The 'must' may be bolded in a browser. But when reading the HTML document out loud by a text-to-speech program, it can be spoken with importance or seriousness.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">&lt;i&gt; vs &lt;em&gt;</p>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; font-style:italic; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; font-style:italic; ">Italics</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span>slants text. We usually italicize names of magazine, books, TV shows etc. Just like the bold tag, since it is meant purely for presentation purposes, it means nothing to someone who cannot read the text.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; font-style:italic; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; font-style:italic; ">Emphasis</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span>is used to stress emphasis of its contents. The word in a sentence you emphasize can change the whole meaning. Try reading the sentences below out loud, stressing on the emphasized words: 'you' and 'store'. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-style:italic; ">You</span> have to go to the store.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>                    Not me. That’s your job! </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> You have to go to the <span style="font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-style:italic; ">store.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>                    To the store. Not the arcade.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Changes in HTML5</p>
			<div>
				<p>So far, we have looked at how these tags were in HTML4. In the beginning of this unit, we learned that content and style should be kept separate and that styling should be kept tucked away in Cascading Style Sheets. So how did <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;i&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;b&gt;</span>, purely style elements make the cut? </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>They were initially deprecated, however, in HTML5, they were brought back. This time, with semantic meaning. </p>
			</div>
			<table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:18.861cm; align:center; margin-left:-.132cm; margin-bottom:0cm">
				<tr style="margin:0;border:0;padding:0;visibility:hidden;">
					<th style="width:43.333px;"/>
					<th style="width:276.867px;"/>
					<th style="width:392.667px;"/>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.184cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:.864cm;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;i&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Apart from italic text, it is now also used for text in a different mood or voice, such as foreign words, a thought or technical terms.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;p&gt;This restaurant has a breakfast buffet and a four course <span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF3300; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;i lang="fr"&gt;</span>À la carte<span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF3300; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;/i&gt;</span> dinner.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.496cm; ">
