					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:.864cm;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;b&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Apart from bolded text, it is now also used as a stylistic offset such as keywords in a document, product names or action words without making them as important. It can also be used as headings in list items.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;p&gt;The owner of this <span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF3300; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;b&gt;</span>rabbit<span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF3300; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;/b&gt;</span>and <span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF3300; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;b&gt;</span>hamster<span style="font-weight:bold; color:#FF3300; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; ">&lt;/b&gt;</span> needs to step forward.&lt;/p&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
			</table>
			<div>
				<p>As of HTML5, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span> is now also used for words and sentences you would pronounce differently. It is not used to convey importance. For that you should use <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span>. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can nest both <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span>. Two &lt;em&gt; means higher level of stress/emphasis on the content than one <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You should also bear in mind that <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;b&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;i&gt;</span> may not produce appropriate styling for some parts of the world. For example, Chinese characters are so complicated that they often prefer something such as underlining to bold, because bold makes it too difficult to read the text.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you do use <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;b&gt;</span> or <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;i&gt;</span> tags, the HTML5 specification recommends that you also use class attributes to identify the semantic intention of the markup. This can be particularly important for pages that get translated, since styling doesn't necessarily map to the same semantic categories across different cultures. For more information, read the article <a href="https://www.w3.org/International/questions/qa-b-and-i-tags"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDWR0L2Z3C4CMPPWP2IZB3RQEXMNJVVEROLUKPDMK1FJWDXBRCU3C">Using &lt;b&gt; and &lt;i&gt; elements</span></span></a>.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.3.2 Introduction to Semantic Elements</p>
			<div>
				<p>Semantic HTML is HTML that concentrates on the meaning of information in Web pages instead of its presentation or look.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">What are semantic elements?</p>
			<div>
				<p>If you want to add a paragraph, you would use the paragraph tag. If you want to add a heading, you would use the header tags <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span>-<span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h6&gt;</span>, and to add an image, you<span>
					</span>would use the image tag (we will learn about this later in this module). All these tags along with their id and class attributes are semantic because they suggest the purpose of the content within the tags. <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;i&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;b&gt;</span> suggest nothing about the content and this is why they were not considered semantic enough and initially deprecated.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Using the right tags</p>
			<div>
				<p>From a semantic HTML perspective, using the right tags is important. You should use <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;blockquote&gt;</span> to wrap a quote and not use a paragraph tag and then style it to look like a quote. You should use <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span> to emphasize a part of your content, not just to italicize text. For presentation purposes, you can achieve the same using CSS. How something looks has very little to do with what it means. This is why in HTML, we separate content and style.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Why is it important?</p>
			<div>
				<p>Semantic elements are beneficial to both the developer and browser. They convey much more information about your HTML document's content and structure. There is a tag called <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">header</span> in semantic HTML. When you see a heading like <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span> or <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h2&gt;</span>, you know this is likely the start of a new sub-section or topic. Communication is always welcome in any programming language.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This additional communication is useful for a <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">developer</span> who can understand the markup structure better (when you come back to your code after a year or pass it on to a colleague, this is going to help you and them a lot!). For the <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">browser</span>, it can better differentiate different types of data which results in better display of content in different devices. <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Assistive technology</span>, such as a screen reader, will read content and convey information about the content depending on the semantic meaning, for example, identifying headers and reading them in a different tone.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Since its establishment, it is an ongoing effort on part of W3C to make HTML as semantic as possible. HTML5 brought with it a slew of new semantic elements.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Web page structure</p>
			<div>
				<p>Let's look at a typical Web page structure that consists of blocks named after: header, nav, article, section, aside and footer.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 29" height="385" width="385" src="module 2_files/image5.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Tags such as<span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> &lt;article&gt;</span>, <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;section&gt;</span>, <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;header&gt;</span>, <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;nav&gt; and &lt;footer&gt; </span>were specifically introduced in HTML5 to define the Web page structure. These new semantic elements give meaning to different parts of a webpage. When you do a Google search, the search engine automatically processes millions of HTML pages to scan and offer you the most appropriate content.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Each section refers to a part of the document:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">header</span> can be a starting point for the whole document or individual sections. It typically contains the introduction.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">nav</span> refers to navigation. It could contain a set of navigation links, such as a table of contents of a book.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">section</span> refers to sections in a document. For example, a document about plants could contain several sections under headings such as perennials, annuals, soil type, etc.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">aside</span> refers to content that is apart from the main content. For example, in an article about a young architect from the Umbria region of Italy. The aside might be a small sidebar with information about Umbria, things like geographical details and population.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">article</span> refers to independent content. If an article is extracted out of the document, it should make sense all by itself. Articles, blog posts, frequently asked questions (FAQ) are all examples of independent content.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">footer</span> contains typical footer information such as authoring, copyrights and contact information.</p>
			<div>
				<p>The use of these semantic elements improves the <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">automated processing of documents</span>. When it scans a <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;nav&gt;</span> tag, it automatically knows it includes content related to page navigation or a header indicates introductory content. It provides the structure and consistent behavior across many webpages providing simpler and more direct information to browsers making life easier for them. It also improves the <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">accessibility</span> of webpages. Assistive technologies depend on the structure of the document to present information to the users. If a screen reader can correctly determine the structure of a document, it reads the document more seamlessly and avoids irrelevant information or repeating content. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We can apply the elements in the image above to a simple Web page like this:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_dec1 style_dec1 " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;html</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">lang</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"en"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;head&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;meta</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">charset</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"UTF-8"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;title&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Introduction to semantic elements</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/title&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/head&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;body&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;header&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Using the Markup Validator.</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/header&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;nav&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_com style_com " style="color:#880000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!--You will learn about &lt;a&gt; tag later in this chapter--&gt;</span></p>
			</div>

				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> One of the important maxims of computer programming is: "Be conservative in what you produce; be liberal in what you accept."</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span></p>
			</div>

The problem is that<span>
						</span></span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">different browsers (or even different versions of the same browser) will make different guesses about the same illegal construct...</span></p>

Did The Validator complain about your DOCTYPE declaration (or lack thereof)? Make sure your document has a syntactically correct DOCTYPE declaration, as described in the section on DOCTYPE, and make sure it correctly identifies the type of HTML you're using. 			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/footer&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/body&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/html&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 30" height="527" width="481" src="module 2_files/image6.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.3.3 New HTML5 Semantic Elements</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">We will elaborate on selected semantic elements in detail in the next unit.</p>
			</div>
			<table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:19.808cm; align:center; margin-left:-.132cm; margin-bottom:0cm">
				<tr style="margin:0;border:0;padding:0;visibility:hidden;">
					<th style="width:149.733px;"/>
					<th style="width:257.133px;"/>
					<th style="width:341.8px;"/>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.413cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p>Semantic Element</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Description</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Example</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.466cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;header&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Introduction for the whole page or individual sections, article, nav, aside elements. Typically contains site name, logo, navigation. Does not have to be at the beginning of page.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;header&gt;<br/>&lt;h1&gt;The Importance of Being Earnest&lt;/h1&gt;<br/>&lt;h3&gt;A Quest for Truth and Beauty&lt;/h3&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;The play was written in 1895 by playwright Oscar Wilde&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/header&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.466cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;footer&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Includes typical footer information like authoring, copyrights, contact information and a footer menu.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;footer&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;Written by: Oscar Wilde&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;Contact information: &lt;a href="mailto:oscar@wilde.com"&gt;<br/>oscar@wilde.com&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/footer&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.466cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;nav&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Navigation links for the document. A page can have more than one &lt;nav&gt; element like table of contents, horizontal navigation in header and footer navigation.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;nav&gt;&lt;ol&gt;<br/>&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="/act1/"&gt;Act 1&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<span style="font-family:inherit; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">  </span><br/><span style="font-family:inherit; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">&lt;li&gt;</span>&lt;a href="/act2/"&gt;Act 2&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br/><span style="font-family:inherit; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">&lt;li&gt;</span>&lt;a href="/act3/"&gt;Act 3&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br/>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/nav&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:2.965cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;section&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Defines sections in the document such as chapters, headers, etc. Typically used on content that cannot make sense on its own. </p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;section&gt;<br/>&lt;h1&gt;Act 1 - Scene 1&lt;/h1&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;Set in the morning room of Algy's flat in Half Moon Street&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/section&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.466cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;article&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Defines independent content that should make sense on its own outside of the document such as newspaper articles, blog posts, etc.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;article&gt;<br/>&lt;h1&gt;A blogger's analysis of this brilliant satire&lt;/h1&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;This witty, sometimes conscious play is Wilde's playground to raise his progressive sentiments...&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/article&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.512cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;aside&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Side content other than main content, like a sidebar. These are not considered as part of the main page outline.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;p&gt;Algernon's flat is luxuriously and artistically furnished&lt;/p&gt;<br/><br/>&lt;aside&gt;<br/>&lt;h3&gt;Algernon Moncrieff&lt;/h3&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;A wealthy bachelor who lives in a fashionable part of London. He has a good sense of humor and utter lack of respect<span>
								</span>for society.&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/aside&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.466cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;details&gt;</span><br/><br/>*see example below</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>A way to provide additional information that the user can show or hide. Content that is shown to user by default. Other content is hidden and can be expanded to view.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;details&gt;<br/>&lt;summary&gt;Cast Members&lt;/summary&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;George Washington as Algernon Moncrieff&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;Ronald Reagan as John Worthing&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/details&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.967cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;figcaption&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
						<div>
							<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">*see example below</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Provides a caption (explanation) of an image. To be used within &lt;figure&gt;.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;figure&gt;<br/>&lt;img src="img_cast.jpg" alt="The Importance of Being Earnest Cast"&gt;<br/>&lt;figcaption&gt;Fig1. - The cast hard at work at dress rehearsal before opening night&lt;/figcaption&gt;<br/>&lt;/figure&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.937cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;figure&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Contains an image and can be used to group with an image's caption</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Refer to &lt;figcaption&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:2.051cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;mark&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
						<div>
							<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">*see example below</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Defines a part of a text you want to highlight. The highlight styling is specified in CSS.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;h4&gt;Lane: &lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Yes sir. [&lt;mark&gt;Handing his master the sandwiches on a salver&lt;/mark&gt;]&lt;/p&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.466cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:3.316cm;">
						<div>
							<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; font-size:10pt; ">&lt;summary&gt;</span></p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Used within the &lt;details&gt; tag. Specifies the visible content. The rest of the content in details is shown/hidden by user.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;details&gt;<br/>&lt;summary&gt;Cast Members&lt;/summary&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;George Washington as Algernon Moncrieff&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;p&gt;Ronald Reagan as John Worthing&lt;/p&gt;<br/>&lt;/details&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
			</table>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">&lt;details&gt; element</p>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;details&gt;</span> tag is very cool. It is used in conjunction with a nested <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;summary&gt;</span> tag and some other content. The result is that the summary is shown with a disclosure triangle alongside it, and the other content is initially hidden.  By clicking the triangle, the other content is displayed to the user. This requires no JavaScript and is a simple way to get a powerful and desirable feature.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Below we see the HTML, and you can try it out for yourself! Note that the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;details&gt;</span> tag works in most Web browsers.</p>
			</div>
			<table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:16.852cm; align:left; margin-left:-.026cm; margin-bottom:0cm">
				<tr style="margin:0;border:0;padding:0;visibility:hidden;">
					<th style="width:434.533px;"/>
					<th style="width:202.4px;"/>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:.531cm; ">

						<div>
							<p>HTML</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:middle; padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#EEEEEE; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:5.355cm;">
						<div>

						<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l2 style_l2 " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
							<span style="font-family:Courier New; color:#454545; padding-right:20px;">3.</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:10.5pt; ">   </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:10.5pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:10.5pt; ">George Washington as Algernon Moncrieff</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:10.5pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>

			<div>
				<p>Element</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>
					<img style="" alt="Picture 32" height="223" width="385" src="module 2_files/image7.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; ">See also the current </span><a href="https://caniuse.com/#search=%3Cdetails%3E"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; "><span class="IDO1F4QPEA4FCPIXMPZIGUNJQYHEZJONXDENOEX5DFXBEOPW5NAFEF">browser support</span></span></a><span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; "> (on caniuse.com).</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">&lt;figcaption&gt; element</p>
			<div>
				<p>This element is used to provide a caption or explanation of the image (figure). While the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute explains the image for assistive technology, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;figcaption&gt;</span> can be used to provide additional information for all users.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;figure&gt;</span></p>
			</div>

			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">Result:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 31" height="193" width="193" src="module 2_files/image8.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/><br/>Fig. 1: The cast hard at work at dress rehearsal before opening night</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">&lt;mark&gt; element</p>
			<div>
				<p>This element is used to specify content that you want to highlight. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Lane: </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Yes sir. [</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;mark&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Handing his master the sandwiches on a salver</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/mark&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">]</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 33" height="223" width="385" src="module 2_files/image9.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Most browsers will display mark element with a yellow background to black text by default, however, if it doesn't, you can specify the styling in CSS. See also the current <a href="https://caniuse.com/#feat=html5semantic"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; "><span class="IDGRPPTDWMZ31TIKLNEYLB5DVE2I2P2F1OPJUXLNNRZW2QBMEWWZQF">browser support</span></span></a> (on caniuse.com).</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Effect of semantic elements</p>
			<div>
				<p>If you have had a chance to try the examples of the semantic elements discussed above, you will notice that semantic elements are not visually promising in general. Only a few semantic elements such as <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;mark&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;code&gt;</span> provide some kind of visual change to the document. The rest don't do anything except providing the structure for your document. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>A good example is <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;aside&gt;</span>. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;aside&gt;</span> element is used for side content other than the main content, such as a sidebar, but it does not actually create a sidebar in your page. Sidebar is a user interface (UI) element and must be styled to achieve the look of a sidebar. The following code will only create structure to your document, not any visual change:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;html lang="en"&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;head&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;meta charset="UTF-8"&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;title&gt;Effect of semantic elements&lt;/title&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;/head&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;body&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;article&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;header id="intro"&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;h2&gt;Introduction&lt;/h2&gt; </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;/header&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;p&gt;HTML5 stands for ...&lt;/p&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;!--This is an example of aside. The mark element has also been showcased in the paragraph --&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;aside&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;h4&gt; API &lt;/h4&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;p&gt; API stands ... &lt;/p&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;/aside&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> &lt;/article&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; ">&lt;/body&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 34" height="247" width="289" src="module 2_files/image10.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Lesser known semantic elements (OPTIONAL)</p>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; ">Note:</span> This section is optional material included for the curious. It will not appear on any graded question.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We will look at a few more semantic elements that are commonly in use but lesser known. </p>
			</div>
			<table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:18.408cm; align:center; margin-left:-.132cm; margin-bottom:0cm">
				<tr style="margin:0;border:0;padding:0;visibility:hidden;">

					<th style="width:327.8px;"/>
					<th style="width:270.6px;"/>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.789cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Semantic Element</p>
						</div>

						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
						<div>
							<p>Example</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.789cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:auto;">
