				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;header id="features"&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;h2&gt;Features&lt;/h2&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;h4&gt;Keeping up with times&lt;/h4&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;/header&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;p&gt;HTML5 introduced elements and attributes that fits the typical usage in modern websites. It introduced new semantic elements to replace generic blocks like div and span. Purely presentation elements such as font and center have also been completely dropped...&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;h4&gt;New APIs&lt;/h4&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;p&gt;New APIs were introduced to allow cross-document communication, drag and drop functionality, immediate mode 2D drawing using the canvas element, webstorage etc...&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;h4&gt;Error Handling&lt;/h4&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;p&gt;HTML5 provides detailed rules for parsing allowing HTML5 compliant browsers to produce the same type of behavior when parsing incorrect syntax. It has been designed for compatibility with older browsers. Older browsers ignore new HTML5 constructs... &lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span></p>
			</div>

				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;/main&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!--Our global footer where you would typically specify copyright, author, contact info and a footer navigation bar--&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;footer&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;p&gt;Copyrights information...&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>

Expand to show content. --&gt;</span></p>
			</div>

			</div>

			</div>

			</div>

				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;p&gt;Author2&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>

			</div>

				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;nav&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!-- Styling has been added to make nav menu in a horizontal row--&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;ul style="margin: 0; padding: 0; list-style-type: none;"&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;li style="display: inline;"&gt;&lt;a href="#" style="text-decoration: none; padding: .2em 1em;"&gt;email&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>

				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;/ul&gt;</span></p>

			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> &lt;/details&gt;</span></p>

				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/body&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/html&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">It is an example of an informational page about HTML5 using the following semantic elements: header, nav, main, article, section, aside, mark, figure, figcaption, details and summary.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Experiment with the sample and try inserting other semantic elements that you want to try.</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.3.6 &lt;div&gt; and &lt;span&gt; Elements</p>
			<div>
				<p>&lt;div&gt; element</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span> tag is one you will likely see sprinkled all over an HTML document.  <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span>, as the Content Division element, is used to define a division or a section of the document. Div is not a semantic element, however, it is commonly used when there isn't a better semantic sectioning element to use.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It is like a <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">generic container</span> that can hold a variety of elements such as paragraphs, images, links, tables, etc. It can be used to group elements for styling purposes. You can do this by assigning an <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> or <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> attribute to the div element and then applying styles which will affect all elements in the div container.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It should only be used if you cannot use any other semantic element in its place.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We will see an example of <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span> here:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;section&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Week 1</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">This week, you will be learning about...week 1 stuff</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;div</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"code"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">    &lt;ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">      &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Line of code</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">      &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Line of code</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">    &lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;/div&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/section&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;section&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Week 2</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">This week, you will be learning about...week 2 stuff</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;div</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"code"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">    &lt;ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">      &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Line of code</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">      &lt;li&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Line of code</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/li&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">    &lt;/ol&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">  &lt;/div&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/section&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you want to style all code snippets in your HTML document a certain way, you can place your code in a div container and apply styles collectively to it using the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>&lt;span&gt; element</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>While we are on the topic of the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span> tag and semantic elements, one more important element that comes in handy is <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span>. Span and Div are so similar yet so different that there is an entire <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Span_and_div"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDLVJRWJOZCMNYE3WAOYEVDIRE2IACUUJGOGOQLNNLO3JNVPKTCJZD">wikipedia page</span></span></a> dedicated to it.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Usage</p>
			<div>
				<p>What happens when you do not find an appropriate tag to use? Let's look<span style="font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; "><span><span></span>
						</span></span>at this example:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Hi everyone! My name is Alexa and I work for ABC Company</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I want to change the color of only 'ABC Company'? Should I use a paragraph tag? Let's try that..</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Hi everyone! My name is Alexa and I work for </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> class</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">company</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">ABC Company</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you then design your style such that the 'company' class will make text blue, the output will look like this:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Hi everyone! My name is Alexa and I work for</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">ABC Company</p>
			<div>
				<p>That does not work because <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt;</span> creates a new line. The HTML above is also invalid. We will see why shortly. Now, let's try using <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span>:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Hi everyone! My name is Alexa and I work for </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;span</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> class="company"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">ABC Company</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Hi everyone! My name is Alexa and I work for <span style="font-family:inherit; color:#0000FF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">ABC Company</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>When can &lt;span&gt; be used?</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>when adding styling to part of a sentence (inline),</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>when manipulating part of a sentence using JavaScript,</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>When there isn't a more appropriate HTML element that applies, you can use <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> (and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span>) to add attributes such as <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">class</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span></p>
			<div>
				<p>Like <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> is not a semantic element. You should only use <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> if no other semantic element is appropriate. <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> serve the same purpose but should be applied at different levels. <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span> is a block level element (for a block of space) while <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> is an inline element (for within a line or phrase).</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Difference between &lt;div&gt; and &lt;span&gt;</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>They are both considered generic elements that don't have any meaning. But <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span> is a block level element while <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> is an inline element. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Block level elements</span> - used within body of the page. These occupy a block of space and start in a new line. They usually have empty lines above and below the block. They can contain inline elements and other block level elements. Other examples: <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span> - <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h6&gt;</span>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Inline elements </span>- as the name suggests are 'in-the-line'. They can start anywhere in a line. They can only contain data (like text) or other in-line elements. Other examples: <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;em&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;strong&gt;</span>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Note: </span>There are several other semantic inline elements such as <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;abbr&gt;</span>, <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;cite&gt;</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;code&gt;</span> that should be used in preference to <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> where possible.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Why two paragraph tags don't work</p>
			<div>
				<p>In the first <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span> example, we said that nesting two paragraph elements was invalid HTML.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">Hi everyone! My name is Alexa and I work for </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;p</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "> class="company"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">ABC Company</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>After reading an opening tag <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt;</span>, if the browser sees another <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt;</span> or any other block level element including <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span>, it will automatically close the first open <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;p&gt;</span> for you. Nesting one paragraph tag in another is not valid because the browser will consider them as two paragraphs one after the other. Even though you close the paragraphs with two closing tags <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span> at the end, they are ignored.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.3.7 Activities – Semantic Meaning</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Please find below suggested activities to help you practice:</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">1.</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">How are </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;header&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; "> and </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; "> related? What is the difference between them?</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">2.</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">Create a well structured HTML page using as many semantic elements as you can.</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">3.</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">Write a short HTML page that uses the </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;div&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; "> and </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;span&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; "> tags. You need not style them.</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.4.1 Introduction</p>
			<div>
				<p>The &lt;img&gt; tag</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this age of visual culture, what is a Web page without images? Boring! Pictures and images make everything more interesting and engaging. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here is the most basic <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img&gt;</span> tag:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"example.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"Example Tutorial Image"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The image tag has several attributes out of which only <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">src</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> are required. The rest are useful but optional attributes. </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true"><span style="font-style:italic; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-size:14pt; font-weight:bold; font-style:italic; ">Image</span>: 'src' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>The source attribute from the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img&gt;</span> tag tells us where to fetch the image from. There are two different types of URLs you can give for source. </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Courier New; color:#454545; padding-right:20px;">1.</span>Path to an image file within your Web site:<br/><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">"images/image-with-relative-url.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">"Example Tutorial Image"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">2.</span>Path to an image file that resides elsewhere on the Web:<br/><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; ">"https://www.example.com/image-with-absolute-</span>url.png" alt="Example Tutorial Image"&gt;</p>
			<div>
				<p>The type of image file format (i.e. png, jpeg, etc.) you should use does not depend on the img element in HTML5 but on the browser that renders the content. Some formats like png, jpeg, gif and bmp are widely supported by browsers and so they are recommended when using images in your Web site. Here is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_web_browsers#Image_format_support"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDNWVLDY2AMUTKCBER0H1SHUOOSFNJ3GD3ZNULHAKTFYRAKQMTMJEJ">comprehensive list by Wikipedia</span></span></a> listing browsers and the image formats they support.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here is a list of things to keep in mind when using the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">src</span> attribute:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Do not include spaces in your image path.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Make sure your image path matches the capitalization of the actual path. Your images directory in your Web project might be 'Images/' but your path might say 'images/' missing the capitalization in 'I'. Mismatched capitalization might work in some places but not all. <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Recommended practice</span>: use lower case for all directories, file names and file extensions.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Use Unix (/) path name separator instead of Windows (\) style. This might work on Windows but will fail elsewhere. The path should be 'images/example.png' and not 'images\example.png'.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>When your Web page loads, it is always going to look at the location you specified in <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">src</span> for the image. Ensure the image resides in the right location or the user is going to get a broken link. This is even more crucial when you use a relative path - any path that is 'relative to' the file. E.g. 'images/test.png' is going to look for the 'images' directory in the same level as your html page. Thus, you need to ensure your document root doesn't change. The simplest is to always keep the images at the same level, or one level down.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Absolute paths are not recommended to use because essentially, you are hardcoding the entire URL. The URL contains parts to it before the actual path - <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; ">https://example.com/images/test.png</span> like the protocol (http) and domain name (example.com). Whereas, relative URLs start with a path - '/images/test.png'. The base URL here comes from where your HTML document is deployed. This is easier to maintain. It will work on localhost or if you switch domain names without requiring any changes.</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-size:14pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-size:14pt; font-weight:bold; ">Image: Formats</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Before you begin using images in your Web site, you are advised to visit this <a href="https://www.smartbugmedia.com/blog/image-file-formats"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDZS4DJU3CXSZ4FTLCGOWYMMNDTIPPF4B4KCRYWZORAPDORBJG3TBC">Web page</span></span></a> to get an understanding of the most common image file types such as jpeg, gif, bmp, tiff and png, their pros and cons, and when to use them.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>When using images in your HTML5, there are a few image format related information to be aware of.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Image data:</span> most images, especially JPEG, contain a lot more data than is needed for a browser and are too often overly large and slow.  You can reduce the size of the image using photo editing software that allows you to re-sample an image to reduce its pixel data and in turn reducing image size. However, once you re-sample an image, do not make change its size (height and width) to make it larger as it will become pixelated and blurry.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">JPEG</span> (Joint Photographic Experts Group) images compress well and are the standard for photos. But they don’t support any sort of animation or transparency.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">PNG</span> (Portable Network Graphics) images support transparency and alpha channels. This makes them useful for non-rectangular images that may need to overlay different background colors or other elements on the page. To make PNG images, a user would need graphics editing software (like GIMP, Photoshop, or others). PNG is a <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/PNG/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDQGEVC2ZRKYQVKL03NEFSZJVVWKNZV5UAOR4XEHDE2RUXBSGATCRB">W3C Web standard</span></span></a> (this is the 2nd edition - the 1st edition was <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/REC-png-961001"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID4I5MTHBGMKWWJCK3BRPKKNVLAL2OQNIWKSFYCBIWL5KCPYCNT0ZE">published</span></span></a> in 1996!).</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">SVG</span> (Scalable Vector Graphics) are defined mathematically and support animation. Also, since they are defined mathematically they scale to <img style="" alt="Picture 42" height="71" width="71" src="module 2_files/image18.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/>any size without worrying about pixels, resolution or image data. This makes SVG images an excellent format to use, if possible. SVG is great for charts, graphs, maps, geometric shapes, and line based illustrations.  SVG is also a markup language in its own right and is very similar to HTML. Typically, it is created with vector graphic software (like<span>
				</span>Inkscape, Adobe Illustrator, and <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/SVG/Tutorial/Tools_for_SVG"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDMDQDEZMDZV34E1HMVZJE3CQ2KCUUIZMWIL2YMVOTKG2PQG5Z4PED">others</span></span></a>), but some people write the markup by hand. Note that SVG 1.1 is a <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/SVG/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDRX5EUY55WIZ1D2AI0HQLEX3NRIX2WHU1JU5Q2ZKF0IPFS3Q2YTQD">W3C Web standard</span></span></a>.</p>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.4.2 Attribute alt</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> stands for <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">alternate text</span> for an image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"image/example.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"Add a short text description of the image here"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Using this attribute, you can provide a short description of what the image is about. This description should convey information about the image or its function in the page. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> is an important attribute because it is the text alternative to the image for users who are unable to see the image, instead using assistive technology like screen readers that rely on the alt text.  It is also useful to provide relevant information for search engines. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Importance of the 'alt' attribute</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you add <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> to your image, screen readers will typically announce that there is an image and read out the contents of the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Your image will not display if the path in your source attribute is wrong, if you have a slow internet connection, or if the image has been relocated or renamed. It will show a broken link. It is useful to have the alternate text display so the user can make sense of the missing image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Search engines do not 'see' images. They rely on the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute to find out what the image is about. If you use your target keyword in <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span>, it will optimize the search.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To consume less data, some mobile users turn off images. They need the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute to find out what the image is about.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> also contributes to semantic meaning - it offers meaning to the image and suggests the purpose of the image content.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If the image is purely for presentation or decoration purposes, you should leave alt empty - <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img alt=""&gt;</span>. Assistive technology will then ignore this content.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Purpose of the image</p>
			<div>
				<p>You can use images for various reasons in your Web page like:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>represent a concept, illustration or just a photograph that provide information</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>background for a button or link</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>display a quote or message in the form of text in an image</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>decorative images</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Depending on the category the image fits into, the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> text differs. This W3C <a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/tutorials/images/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDASQ0BNTHX20XHEIMF3CRLAXQWCIHIM3RVV4HDSPWFVPUJHI4KK0I">WAI Images Tutorial</span></span></a> is an excellent resource for deciding the category of your image and for learning how to write proper alt text for that category.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here is an example of a tulip image using invalid source (that image is missing from the 'images' directory) and how it will look in a Web browser:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift;
