font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"image/tulips.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"This is supposed to be an image of tulips"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 43" height="245" width="385" src="module 2_files/image19.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.4.3 Attributes: title, height &amp; width</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">The 'title' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>Try this: place your mouse on the image below. Don't click, just rest your cursor on it. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 46" height="226" width="301" src="module 2_files/image20.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Did you see the hidden message 'Tulips from woodburn tulip festival'? <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span> is a global attribute we have seen before but worth mentioning again because it is very<span>
					</span>useful in an <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img&gt;</span> tag. If you have a complicated image that could use a tooltip or description, you will want to use the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span> attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"images/tulips.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"This is supposed to be an image of tulips"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">title</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"Tulips from woodburn tulip festival"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute is meant to be an alternate source of information while the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span> attribute should provide additional information about the image. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Note</span>: For images, you <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">must</span> use an <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute as there is no guarantee that the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span> attribute is presented to assistive technology users. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">title</span> attribute should not be relied upon for important information, and it should not be used in place of the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span> attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The 'height' &amp; 'width' attributes</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Not all your images come in the right size for your Web page. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">width</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">height</span> attributes can be used to resize the image in pixels without using an external editor.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here is my original image:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 45" height="292" width="193" src="module 2_files/image21.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Clearly too big for the page. The original image dimensions is 345x523 in pixels. Pixel is short for picture element. These are the little dots that make up your image on a computer display like the monitor or laptop you are viewing this in. Pixels are generally too small to see (unless you look really close) and a screen might be made up of millions of pixels.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, if I want to resize the HTML logo above by half:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"images/html5.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"HTML resized image"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">title</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"Resized image seems to fit the page better"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">height</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"173"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">width</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"262"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 44" height="146" width="96" src="module 2_files/image22.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Actually, you don't need to define both <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">width</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">height</span>. You can just specify either <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">height</span> or <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">width</span> and the aspect ratio will be adjusted. For example, the image above can be achieved using the following too:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;img</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"images/html5.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"HTML resized image"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">title</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"Resized image seems to fit the page better"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">height</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"173"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The use of these attributes really depends on how you are using the image. If it is part of an <a href="https://www.imagely.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/03/adding-functionality-justified-image-grid-03.png"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDL5XSSCMZK5MUHD3GBXDWWUAYNFHQG0PMZ2ASLB3ULMEPOD45MWP">image grid</span></span></a> or a list with multiple images of the same size, it is best achieved by CSS. So you don't have to bother adding the same dimensions to every image and it will be repetitive. Plus it is generally bad practice to encode dimensions directly into the HTML.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>However, if you are adding the image into some content and it needs to be a certain size for the visual flow of the reader, then it is best to add it to HTML using the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">height</span> and <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">width</span> attributes. This is to avoid cluttering your CSS with a style for every image in your page. This is also useful if you are changing or removing the image: you can just remove it from your HTML and not deal with remembering to remove it from your CSS too.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.4.4 Decorative Images</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Should all images be part of HTML content?</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">A significant part of images on the Web are not used for any meaning. They merely serve a decorative purpose and fall under the presentation category. How do you identify these images? Well, if you have nothing relevant to put in your </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">alt</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "> attribute or if you feel like it is not important to your or to the prospective reader, it should not be in your HTML.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">We know we should keep content and style separate in HTML. Then how do we move these images out of content? Well, don't add them using the </span><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;img&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "> tag in HTML. Use CSS instead. </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Examples of such images:</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">background images</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">fancy border graphics</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">banner graphics</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; ">pictures of landscapes or textures that are being used as elements behind or surrounding the content</span></p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Some pages (especially for video games, fancy magazines, etc) have a lot of eye-candy imagery that is not core to any of the semantic meaning of the page.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Can you identify these type</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">s</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "><span><span></span>
						</span>of decorative images?</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Find out from their tooltips!</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 52" height="193" width="193" src="module 2_files/image23.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/>
					<img style="" alt="Picture 51" height="193" width="193" src="module 2_files/image24.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/>
					<img style="" alt="Picture 50" height="193" width="193" src="module 2_files/image25.jpeg" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.4.5 Using &lt;img&gt; Tags</p>
			<div>
				<p>Hi there! In this video, we're going to take a closer look at how we add images to our HTML pages.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We'll explore how to load an image, and how to give it a good alternate text value, and a good title value, as well as how to adjust the size of the image on a page using 'height' and 'width' attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We've all heard the phrase that a picture paints a thousand words.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Well, images are a very important part of any Web page design.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>They enhance the visual appeal of a page, can create excitement or interest about our content, and can have an impact on the message we are sending our readers.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's load our first image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To define an image on a page, we use the image element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now this is a self-closing tag, meaning that it doesn't require an end tag.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To define the image, we go inside the image tag and we set some attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>One of the key attributes to set is the source attribute, which tells the browser the location of the image and before I set this let's have a look at the images on my local machine.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>As you can see my "images.html", which is this page, is here on my local machine.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And at the same level on my desk, I have this "images" folder which is a good practice for gathering all the images I want to use on my web page or Web site into this single folder.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Inside this "images" folder, I have lots of images, some of them are png and jpg files and as you can imagine any modern browser can support these image types and can show the images.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The image I want to use is located in this "images" folder and it's called "beach.png".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's the value I will set here in my HTML page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll set the location to be: "images/beach.png".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's a relative path, it's telling the browser that they'll find this image, in an "images" folder and it's called, beach.png.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>When I "Save" my file, there you go, I have loaded my first image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's talk now about the 'alt' attribute and why we add alternate text.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The 'alt' attribute is important because it offers an alternate source of information about this image for those who cannot see the image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This text is read aloud by screen reader software for those with impaired vision or disabilities.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And search engines can't see the image either, so they rely on the alt text to understand what the image is about.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This text is also displayed to the user if, for some reason, the browser can't display your image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For all of these reasons make sure you supply a good descriptive alt text for every image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now what text you supply depends on the type of image you are displaying.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If the image is just a background or a decorative image, you might not want to describe it with this text and instead let the screen reader skip over it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But for functional images or images containing or supporting information for your page, you should always apply this alt text.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, while the image we have in front of us here could be decorative, what of is being shown on the page that is, renting a beach house, and this is a view from the backyard.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In that case, I would provide a description that conveys the meaning of the image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I think this would be a good alternate attribute value.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here what I've said is:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>"Enjoy the magnificent view of the beach and the sea from this oceanfront cottage."</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's show the alt text in action when the browser can't load my image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To do that, I'm going to break the link on the page by pointing to a location or file that doesn't exist.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For example, if I have a typo here, and that now is a file that doesn't exist on my disk, so as you can see, when the link for the image points to a file that doesn't exist, our alt text is displayed nice and clearly on the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This is the view that you would see.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It's not ideal but at least you still get some information and can continue with the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's the alt text attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's go ahead and repair our link so we can see the image again.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll just change it back to the original value, and I'll move this down so we can see it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So the next attribute that I'd like to talk to you about is the 'title' attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now this is a global attribute and it's supported by the image element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It's used to convey more information about the image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For example, if I type in, 'title=' and then paste in some descriptive text it says, "Oceanfront view from the Surfers Paradise rental cottage, California."</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And what happens is, if I sav my page, nothing looks like it happened over on the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But if I hover over the actual image, now I get that information.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This is a visual element that is displaying more information about the actual image in question.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's the 'title' attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now let's have a look at how you adjust the size of the image on our page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For that I'm going to need a bigger image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To save time I'll just "Paste" in a new image and "Save" my page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And as you can see this is a new image, smiley.jpg and if I scroll down you can see whooo, this is a very large image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What can we do?</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Well we can easily fix this with the help of the 'width' and 'height' attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>While I use this attribute 'width', I'll have to define this in pixels.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You may have heard the term pixel before.<span>
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It's just a unit of measurement for computer screens.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Each screen is made up of millions of these tiny squares called pixels.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For example, my monitor that you see here is 1920 by 1080, meaning it's a thousand nine hundred and twenty pixels tall and a thousand eighty pixels wide.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's try 'width' value in pixels and I'll pick something small.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Say, 300, and I'll "Save" my image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And after I just scroll down you can see my image is actually showing.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Again if I remove the 'width', "Save" again, you can see the image is in its native size but if I was to set the 'width', you can see the image shrinks down to a nice size.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You also notice that I've only defined a new 'width' attribute value but the height of the image has also been adjusted.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Well that's because the browser tries to maintain the aspect ratio of the image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I could define a 'height' attribute as well.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And when I "Save" my image, when I scroll down you can see that the image height has changed and the image looks squashed because I've changed the aspect ratio, the height to width ratio.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll just remove that once more, and there we have a smaller image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's changing the size of an image using the 'width' and 'height' attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Finally, I'd like to show you how to load remote images.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Up until this point we've loaded images located on a path relative to our page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>As you can see here the smiley.jpg image is in a folder called "images" relative to this page called images.html</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>However, the real power of the Web is to be able to gather information from across the Internet.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And all we need to do is supply an address.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This time, I'll "Paste" one in and as you can see, this is just a URL and it's telling the browser to find this image located at this site and gist.githubsercontent.com/AndrewJburn, etc., etc.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>At the end of this long URL is just the name of my image, image001/png.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And when I "Save" my file and we scroll down, you can see that that image has been loaded from this remote site into our Web page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So, that's it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this video, we had fun with images, the image tag and its attributes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You're all set to spice up your pages with some images. Take care!</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.4.6 Activities - Images</p>
			<div>
				<p>Please find below a list of possible activities:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">1.</span>Create a simple Web page that talks about your day using only text and images. Include at least three images and add the <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:12pt; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:12pt; ">alt</span> and <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:12pt; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:12pt; ">title</span> attributes. </p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">2.</span>Look through the Web and your favorite Web sites and identify those that you think use a lot of decorative images.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="padding-right:20px;">3.</span>Create a HTML page and add the following types of images:<br/>- Informative image that represents concepts and information<br/>- Decorative image<br/>- Images of text</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; ">Use the alt attribute to provide alternate text for the images above. <br/>Refer to the <a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/tutorials/images/">WAI Images Tutorial</a> for a guide to writing alternate text. </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.5.1 Introduction</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">What are hyperlinks?</p>
			<div>
				<p>In a typical Web page, you may well have seen a sentence like this one:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>
					<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-style:italic; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; font-style:italic; "><span class="IDSU34E1MZDFHPJ2X10RTV4THRYL40WOCW1C0CGQGDZQ1WWMWAPQJN">Find out more</span></span></a><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> about our offers! </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Or something like this:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb " style="text-align:center; ">
					<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships">
						<img style="" alt="Picture 53" height="44" width="232" src="module 2_files/image26.png"/>
					</a> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Try clicking the blue text or the 'Buy Now!' button, if you haven't already (make sure to navigate back to the course).</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>A hyperlink is any text or image that takes you to another place. This can be:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>another Web page: e.g. the hyperlinks wiki page at <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>a bookmark (a specific part of a Web page): e.g. the History section of the Hyperlinks wiki page at <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink#History</span><span style="font-weight:bold; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; "><br/></span><br/>We learned about using the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute as a link target in the unit about attributes earlier. If you have a section in your page, you can link to that section using the value of its <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">id</span> attribute (e.g. History) preceded by the number sign as per <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Emphasis style_Emphasis " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-style:italic; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">#History</span></p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>a local link (link to another part of the same Web page): e.g. <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Courier New; ">a_tag.asp</span> is a page that belongs to this Web site</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>an email: e.g. mailto:helloauthor@w3c.com</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Why you should prefer text links over images</p>
			<div>
				<p>When it comes to hyperlinks, try to use text instead of images when possible.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Images are not as well understood or recognized as text.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Text is better for accessibility.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>If you have text in an image like the 'Buy now' button, search engines do not recognize text in images. The text alternative for the image should convey the action that will be initiated (the purpose of the image, e.g, "buy now"), rather than a description of the image ("button").</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Best practices</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Apply hyperlinks to short phrases. It is unusual to see the link tag used around a whole paragraph.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Make link phrase meaningful. Avoid phrases like 'Click Here' or 'Read More'. 'Click here to get help' is redundant when you can create a link around the phrase 'Get Help'. The link is an indication that it should be clicked.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Don't use short link text. It is easy to miss the 'blue' hyperlink if it is used on one word or character and is hard for users to click using touch screen.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Appearance - links have a default appearance in most browsers, blue and underlined. Ensure no other text in your page is underlined so as to avoid confusing the user. They might get frustrated trying to click text that they think is a link.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>If you choose to have image links, it should have <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">alternate text</span> that describes the purpose of the link instead of the image used - describe the target link.</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">"https://www.table-header-cells.com"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l1 style_l1 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; ">src</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">"table-th.png"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">"Introduction to table header cells and their usage"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l2 style_l2 " style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">Anchor element</p>
			<div>
				<p>The hyperlink tag in html is simply <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Courier New; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Courier New; font-size:13.5pt; ">&lt;a&gt;,</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span>and it is called the<span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> anchor element</span>. Here is how it is used:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Click here</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> to go to the Wikipedia Hyperlink page.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Result: </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; font-weight:bold; color:WindowText; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; font-weight:bold; "><span class="IDGHOZISROD55KBEJJ5342DM4MIMKHBMWFQKHPVRIC1OPZFM03UOSE">Click here</span></span></a><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; "> to go to the Wikipedia Hyperlink page.</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Note: The anchor element should not be confused with the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;link&gt;</span> tag. The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;link&gt;</span> tag is used to define a link between a document and an external resource like an external style sheet. You will learn more about the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;link&gt;</span> tag in the next chapter.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">States of a hyperlink</p>
			<div>
				<p>If the link has not been clicked, it will be blue and underlined. Now, click on the link and you will see that a visited link looks purple and underlined. Apart from unvisited and visited links, there is also a status called active link. A link becomes active while the user is clicking on it. During this time, the link will be red and underlined.</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Unvisited</span>: blue + underlined</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Visited</span>: purple + underlined</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Active</span>: red + underlined</p>
			<div>
				<p>Usage</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;a&gt;</span> tag can surround text or an image. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_com style_com " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!-- Text in a hyperlink--&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">If you click on me, I will take you to qwant.com</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_com style_com " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!-- Paragraph in a hyperlink--&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"https://www.qwant.com/"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">If you click on me, I will take you to qwant.com</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_com style_com " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!-- Image in a hyperlink--&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">alt</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can even use the anchor element to add your email address under the contacts section of your Web page.<span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_HTMLCode style_HTMLCode " style="font-size:13.5pt; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:10pt; font-size:13.5pt; "> </span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">Feedback: </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt;
