">"mailto:authors@example.com"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">Send Mail to Authors</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Result (try the hyperlink below):</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Feedback: <a href="mailto:authors@example.com"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID1EQZZY332O2FOVAMX24X3GENXDVBVXNHR4W0GWIHCLPWMNQYLWKG">Send Mail to Authors</span></span></a>
				</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can add a subject to the email. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">Feedback: </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">"mailto:authors@example.com?Subject=Hello"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">Send Mail to Authors with Subject</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Result (try the hyperlink below)</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Feedback: <a href="mailto:authors@example.com?Subject=Hello"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDQM0L1BIZMSDNJKLRRU52LXLZDDOONV4CQNCWZKEL0DSJ3NWV2CLJ">Send Mail to Authors with Subject</span></span></a>
				</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Nevertheless, you should probably avoid using hyperlinks for email addresses:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>The email address usually opens up on the default email client on the user's computer which they might not use. This defeats the whole purpose.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>Providing your email address in your Web page directly as text or a hyperlink will expose your email address. Bots or spam crawlers can be used to search the Web to pick up email addresses for spam. You should avoid this if possible and use contact forms instead.</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.5.2 Attributes: href and target</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">The 'href' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>The only attribute we have seen thus far in this chapter of hyperlinks is <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">href</span>. <br/><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">href</span> points to the URL that the link should jump to. Though it is an optional attribute, without it, the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">&lt;a&gt;</span> tag will not be a hyperlink because it obviously has no idea where to jump to.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">href</span> attribute takes a URL. This URL can be in the form of:</p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>a link to an external Web site also known as <a href="https://www.differencebetween.com/difference-between-an-absolute-and-vs-a-relative-url/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDFFRGOPP5K4PWPOFPO5YK0LCYRJ14KVU30J4QBFONU2CB0WKG32JI">absolute URL</span></span></a>.</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:48px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">"https://qwant.com"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>a link to a file or page within the same Web site also known as <a href="https://www.differencebetween.com/difference-between-an-absolute-and-vs-a-relative-url/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDHYZKZDDKEQK5B1V5KW3TVAERRKY5TJMARHZKWWNB0STGM3E5EWPB">relative URL</span></span></a>. </p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:48px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">"contacts.html"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>a link to an element on the same page. The element, is referenced using its ID. E.g. If you want to link to a div with id='details', the corresponding anchor tag will be:</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:48px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">"#details"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_ListParagraph style_ListParagraph " style="margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; margin-left:48px; text-indent:-.635cm; ">
				<span style="font-family:Symbol; padding-right:20px;">·</span>protocols such as:</p>
			<div>
				<p>- mailto: | for email addresses. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:48px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">"mailto:abc@alphabets.com"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:inherit; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true"> </p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">The 'target' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">target</span> specifies the destination where the linked URL in <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">href</span> should be opened. It can take a variety of different values, but for our purposes we'll focus on the two below.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "> </p>
			</div>
			<table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:18.45cm; align:center; margin-left:-.132cm; margin-bottom:0cm">
				<tr style="margin:0;border:0;padding:0;visibility:hidden;">
					<th style="width:275.4px;"/>
					<th style="width:85.667px;"/>
					<th style="width:195.733px;"/>
					<th style="width:140.533px;"/>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:1.951cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:40.32%;">
						<div>
							<p>Destination</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:11.66%;">
						<div>
							<p>Attribute value</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:28.88%;">
						<div>
							<p>Example</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#3D64FF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:19.14%;">
						<div>
							<p>Result (try this)</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:3.884cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:40.32%;">
						<div>
							<p>In the same view where the link resides. If no target is specified, this is the default behavior.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:11.66%;">
						<div>
							<p>_self</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:28.88%;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;a href="<span style="font-family:inherit; color:#339966; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">https://qwant.com/</span>" target="<span style="font-family:inherit; color:#339966; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">_self</span>"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:19.14%;">
						<div>
							<p>
								<a href="https://qwant.com/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:10.5pt; "><span class="IDSZNNTN3CTC2UIEJ4STJ3E0KTVEHOUFG2H2CY0RPWEHUIYB3PIB1F">LINK will open in same window</span></span></a> (Navigate back to the course by clicking Back button in browser)</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
				<tr style="height:5.674cm; ">
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:40.32%;">
						<div>
							<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb ">In a new window or tab. This is very convenient if you want to link the user to a Web page without having the current page disappear. By clicking on the previous window or tab, they can redirect to the page where the link is.</p>
						</div>
						<div>
							<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_NormalWeb style_NormalWeb "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:10.5pt; ">Note: </span>It is best to inform users that the page will open in a new tab or window when using '_blank' as some may not be aware of the new tab having opened.</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:11.66%;">
						<div>
							<p>_blank</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:28.88%;">
						<div>
							<p>&lt;a href="<span style="font-family:inherit; color:#339966; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">https://qwant.com/</span>" target="<span style="font-family:inherit; color:#339966; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:inherit; ">_blank</span>"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</p>
						</div>
					</td>
					<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:.265cm; padding-left:.265cm; padding-right:.265cm; padding-top:.265cm; background-color:#FFFFFF; border-left:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-right:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-top:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; border-bottom:solid .026cm #C4C8CB; width:19.14%;">
						<div>
							<p>
								<a href="https://qwant.com/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:10.5pt; "><span class="IDLRVRUHHNC0R0CY42G2D1DTAJIELL4RZNPHN4SKKS30OUMYLHSRGH">LINK will open in new window</span></span></a>
							</p>
						</div>
					</td>
				</tr>
			</table>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.5.3 Attributes: Media and Download</p>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">The 'media' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">media</span> attribute was introduced in HTML5. We will look at it briefly here. It is used to specify what kind of media or device the URL you linked to in <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">href</span> is optimized for. The URL could be targeted for special devices like projectors, speech synthesizers or pages meant to be printed. It is useful if you want to cater your target document that the URL points to a particular device type.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Imagine you have a page scattered with multiple images and you want to display this page on a handheld device. Handheld devices are known to have small screens and limited bandwidth. We want to align the page better for a small screen and reduce the size of images. So the media attribute allows us to tell the anchor element that this page is targeted for handheld devices. You do this by providing a<span>
					</span>value for the attribute. This value could be any valid <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css3-mediaqueries/"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="IDJE2N4IMDDHPZMT5HU0ZYA2AN4VOTSXE2HNCMSLMP2NLVTXOKREE">media query </span></span></a>and is a combination of <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">device type</span> and <span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">media rendering values</span>.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's look at another example - you could create a print link to a long content heavy page that will redirect you to a print version of the same. You want this print version to be formatted into one page ideal for printing and with resolution of 250 dpi. Here is how the HTML5 code will look like:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 " style="margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Media_queries?output=print"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">media</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"print and (resolution:250dpi)"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">Print wiki page about media queries</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-size:11pt; font-family:Consolas; color:#000088; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading3 style_Heading3 " style="outline-width:3; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">The 'download' attribute</p>
			<div>
				<p>The <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">download</span> attribute is also new in HTML5 and it makes a link download a file instead of navigate to another location. It takes in the filename as value but the value is optional. So the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">download</span> attribute can be specified in the following ways:</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"/assets/hello.txt"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">download</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">="</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">/assets/hello.txt" download="</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">new-name-for-text-file</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you do not specify a value for download, it will download the file with name unchanged. Else it will download the file with file name modified according to value specified. </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"/assets/hello.txt"</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">download</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>... will download the file with the same name - 'hello.txt'.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_tag style_tag " style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;a</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pln style_pln " style="color:#000000; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "> </span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">href</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_pun style_pun " style="color:#666600; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">="</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">/assets/hello.txt" download="</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atn style_atn " style="color:#660066; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">new-name-for-text-file</span><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_atv style_atv " style="color:#008800; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>... will download the file after altering its name to - 'new-name-for-text-file.txt'.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Example (try the hyperlink below in Google Chrome): </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>
					<a href="https://courses.edx.org/assets/courseware/v1/6e709b3765de6510e212932331a0bf52/asset-v1:W3Cx+HTML5.0x+3T2020+type@asset+block/hello.txt"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID4I5DUNA2VZX4FAIYXRQFLLNQFJEVII0R3ESUPJM11QUR0L5ZSHGB">Click to Download</span></span></a>
				</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Strong style_Strong " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:Inter; color:#454545; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; font-family:Inter; font-size:13.5pt; ">Note: </span>the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">download</span> attribute is <a href="https://caniuse.com/#search=download"><span class="style_DefaultParagraphFont style_DefaultParagraphFont style_Hyperlink style_Hyperlink " style="font-size:13.5pt; font-family:inherit; color:#00688D; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; text-decoration:underline ;font-family:inherit; font-size:13.5pt; "><span class="ID0DSMVKSGOU3UMG1ECIVGBBFYCGNLB0CWRHPRYMI3G4MSKUTFQWQ">not supported in all browsers</span></span></a>. Try the <span style="font-family:Courier New; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Courier New; ">download</span> attribute in a html file of your own and run it in different browsers to see how it behaves.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.5.4 Use of Hyperlink Attributes</p>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 48" height="263" width="481" src="module 2_files/image27.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this live coding demo, we're going to dive deep into hyperlinks.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Hyperlinks, or links for short, are what give the Internet its magic.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>They allow us to share and connect with other content.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And I'm sure you click on some links on a Web page at least a few times a day.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>For this demo, we have Visual Studio Code open here on the right, and our browser open on the left.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, I'm in the process of creating this page you see before you called "Page 1".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What I'm going to do is use this fictitious page to create hyperlinks and demo all of their features.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's dive right in.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The first thing to do is to show you what my site looks like on disc.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And as you can see, I have two pages, Page 1, Page 2.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I also have this "assets" folder and I'll get to that later.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But for now, you can see I have two pages and it's quite common on a Web site that you want to jump from one page to the other.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And I'm demonstrating that here with "See page 2 for more information."</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What I actually want to do is make that "page 2" words, make those clickable.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>When the user clicks on them, I jump to Page 2.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Enter hyperlinks.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Over here in my HTML code, I'm going to add an anchor element and define the page 'href' attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And there I have defined it as "page2.html".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What I was saying is that when you click on this link, please go to "page2.html".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can see Page 2 is now enclosed inside this anchor element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That will be the hyperlink text and we see that when I save the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And over here you see that's now a hyperlink.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If I click on the hyperlink as a user, I go to Page 2.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>"Hi from Page 2!"</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You may have noticed that when I clicked on this Page 2 hyperlink, Page 1 was replaced with Page 2 in the same tab in my browser.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And that sometimes is not what you want.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Maybe sometimes you want to open up a new tab in your browser, and that's all controlled with this target attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Allow me to demonstrate.<span>
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this next demo, I say, "Open page 2 in a new window."</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here I'm going to make a hyperlink for this new window and when I click, it will open Page 2 but it won't replace this tab with that page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'm going to open a new tab.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To do that, I have to again, define another hyperlink.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It has the same 'href' attribute as the last demo, but this time,</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'm going to use the 'target' property or 'target' attribute", and I'm going to say the target attribute is "_blank".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>There are multiple target attributes you can define, there's "blank" and "self".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>"self" is the default meaning "Open in the same tab.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>"blank" means open in a new tab.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Again, I'll just move my anchor and tag behind my words here, "new window" and when I save my file, you'll see now that "new window" is hyperlinked.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And when I click on it, this time Page 2 will open but watch what happens.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Page 2 is opened in a new tab besides Page 1.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's often the behavior that you want on your Web site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Remember that 'target' attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The next thing I want to show you is how do you link out to a page or a site that's not part of your own Web site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Well, that's very straightforward.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It's practically the same as the last two only instead of a local reference to a page like this "page2.html", we're actually going to enter a location of a page or a site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here and this "Remember to Always Be Learning", I'm going to hyperlink "Always Be learning" and take us somewhere we can maybe take a course.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll again, use my anchor tag and this time, in the 'href' I'll enter a URL to a Web site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now I have my anchor tag defined again, I'll move the end tag to the end of the words I want to hyperlink and I will save that.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Maybe I'll use the target again</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We can see it side by side.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>There I have my target defined as well.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Once I save my html code, you can see that this phrase is now hyperlinked, "Remember to Always Be Learning", and you can see that at the bottom it's telling me the name of the link is, "www.edx.org".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>As you can imagine, when I click this link, I get taken to the edX Web site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now we have three hyperlinks. Let's continue.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this next example, as its name suggests, I'm going to show you how we can get the user to download a file.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's go back to my folder structure on disk.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>As I mentioned, I have this assets folder which is pretty standard in a Web site to have some folders containing assets you may want to download or you might want to use on your site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In here, I have this little file called, "instructions.txt", it's a text file.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What I want to do is I want to get the user to download it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here I have, "Download our instructions on how to be smarter."</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I want to hyperlink, "our instructions" and see how to get that to download.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So back in my Web page here, and my html code, I'm going to add an anchor and I'll say, 'href=' and if I just say, remember it's a relative link to that file on my site, so its "assets/instructions.txt".<span>
					</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's say that's all I enter, "assets/instructions.txt."</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's see what happens. Again, I'll move my end tag and I'll save them.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now we have instructions as a hyperlink, and when I click on that what happens is, it actually shows those instructions in the browser which is not what I wanted.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I wanted to download them.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I wanted the user to download them.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To do that, I just use the 'download' attribute.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Just add that attribute, "Save" my file, "Save" my html and at this time when I click on "instructions", they will ask me, "Do you want to download it?"</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll say, "Yes".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And "View" downloads and there you can see I've downloaded this file.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The next thing I want to do is look at hyperlinks that jump around locally inside your page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Consider this example, where I have something, a lot of text or content and I want to get down here.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I want to give the user the ability to jump past some information maybe or referring them to something else on the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's a local jump on the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What I need to do here in order for this to work is I first have to go down to where I want to jump to.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>In this case, I want to jump to this text which is here on my page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And what I have to do first of all, is I have to set an 'id' on this element.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And here, I'll just give it any 'id' I wish, I'll call it, "important stuff".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Then, I go back up to my page and if I want to hyperlink these words so that when the user clicks, they jump past all this content and down here,</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I need to create a hyperlink.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And this is special hyperlink because it needs to have a special 'href'.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Here I'll add my anchor and this time, I start my 'href' with a "#" which is this symbol here and then the 'id' of the element I want to jump to.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And we named our element, "important stuff".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's my hyperlink, and as usual, I'll move my end tag. And when I save my file, I now have a new hyperlink and when I click on it, watch how the page scrolls.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>It jumps all the way down to "You found me!"</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's how you can do a local hyperlink on a page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That concludes our live coding demo on hyperlinks.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You've seen how to use the attributes on the anchor tag to jump to pages on our site, visit other sites, download files and even skip around on the same page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading2 style_Heading2 " style="outline-width:2; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">2.5.6 Recipe Project – Module 2</p>
			<div>
				<p><span style="background-color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">We are now going to continue building on the recipe project we started in<span>
						</span></span><span style="background-color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; ">Module 1.  You can find our version in the CodePen below (and the live coding</span><span style="background-color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; "><span><span></span>
						</span>video at the end of this page).</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p style="text-align:center; ">
					<img style="" alt="Picture 49" height="243" width="481" src="module 2_files/image28.png" xmlns="http://schemas.openxmlformats.org/package/2006/relationships"/> </p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div>
			<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_Heading5 style_Heading5 " style="outline-width:5; " xmlns:text="urn:oasis:names:tc:opendocument:xmlns:text:1.0" text:is-list-header="true">HTML</p>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;html</span><span style="color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "><span><span></span>
						</span></span><span style="color:#DDCA7E; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">lang</span><span style="color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span style="color:#96B38A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"en"</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;head&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;meta</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; "><span><span></span>
						</span></span><span style="color:#DDCA7E; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">charset</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">=</span><span style="color:#96B38A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">"UTF-8"</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;title&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">My Favorite Recipes - Module 2</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/title&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/head&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;body&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;h1&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">My Favorite Recipes</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/h1&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;nav&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">
					</span><span style="color:#A7925A; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;ul&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="color:#FFFFFF; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">

					</span><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/body&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p class="style_Normal style_Normal style_l0 style_l0 style_NoSpacing style_NoSpacing " style="margin-left:24px; "><span style="font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:11pt; font-family:Bahnschrift; font-size:12.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt; font-family:Consolas; font-size:11pt; ">&lt;/html&gt;</span></p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Hello, everyone. In this live coding demo, we're going to enhance this recipe page that was introduced earlier.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We're going to use lots of tags and attributes that we learned about in this module.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>As you probably guessed, this page is going to describe some of my favorite recipes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>At the moment, as recipe pages go, this is a very bland page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We're going to spruce it up visually and use some semantic tags to assist the visually impaired, as well as you, the developer.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We're not introducing anything new here, we're just going to put together everything we've learned into creating a richer piece of content. Let's get started.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Okay, I have a very rough outline of my first recipe here and clearly, we've a lot of work to do.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The first thing I'm going to do is give this first recipe a title.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>This one is going to be my soup recipe and so I'll display that in a 'h2' heading element, like so.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Every decent recipe book is filled with pictures of culinary delights, so our page should be no different.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>If you look at the "Explore" panel here in Visual Studio, you can see I have an images folder already here for this site.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And if you click on the soup image, you can see that's a nice picture of some delicious soup.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's use that for this particular recipe.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To do that, I'll just close that and come back to my HTML, and I'll use the image tag to define this image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>As you may have seen before, this picture lies in the images folder of our site so it's a relative path, images/soup.jpg.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>After this, I'll add some alt text, as we always recommend: "a nice bowl of soup".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And you can see I have that bowl of soup, those two bowls of soup now showing on my page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>One more thing I want to do here is just to use my width attribute, to make sure that that image sits nicer on the page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I think that looks a lot better.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Great, so now we have an image for our lovely recipe.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>A recipe looks pretty good for now, I'm not going to actually include real ingredients or actual steps in the recipes just for the sake of time, but I will recommend that you look at the description here of the recipe and when you are adding content to a page like this it's always good to have a light voice to your content.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I just paste an example there of something I might write for this.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'm also using the quotation element that we came across before to actually have an inline quote from Beethoven.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>There's some nice content for us to introduce the steps for this particular recipe.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So as the page continues, you can imagine adding more recipes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And so, what I would do here just to save some time, I think what I will do is I'll just copy and paste what we have so far and I'll create more recipes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>The next one might be a salad, and the salad will probably use a salad image.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Makes more sense.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can see that's got a salad image, a nice plate of salad, and the 'width' tag for this image element suits me nicely as well.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll paste in another descriptive piece of content, just so we can have some uniqueness to each of our recipes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I have soup, I have salad.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I think I'll conclude with a nice recipe for pizza.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll change my 'h2' tag, I'll add my pizza image, "A warm pizza pie".</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And then I will add in some text about this to the recipe.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And when I scroll down, you can see now I have three recipes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Each one comes with an image, ingredients, little bit of content, and some steps to create these wonderful meals.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's what the recipe page now looks like and it looks, you'll agree, it looks a lot richer.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And so, we won't do much more with a page from a visual perspective.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>What I'd like to do finally here is just use some semantic tags that will aid not just you, the developer, but also the visually impaired as we move along.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can imagine developing a page like this and as a developer, it's really hard to distinguish between each of the various recipes and the recipes are very standalone, and this means they're a great candidate for the article semantic tags.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll surround each of these recipes with the 'article' semantic tag and I'll do that as follows.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Just above, for example, the soup recipe, I'll just add 'article', click the opening tag, and I'll close it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I'll surround the complete soup recipe with my 'article' tag.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And I'll do the exact same for my salad, and finally for my pizza.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, I have three recipes, each distinguished by an article element inside my page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And I'll save my page, you can see that that has no effect visually at the moment on anything but there could be screen readers that would use this tag in order to help the visually impaired understand the contents of this page, and possibly as well, in a developer environment, these tags may be useful for collapsing and expanding articles in this page content.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And finally, we can use these article tags to extract content that is independent and use it in other sources such as blog posts or on other pages.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>That's the use of the semantic tag called 'article'.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Another thing that may be stand out here is, we have multiple recipes, it might be nice to jump from one recipe to the other or to have a table of contents at the very top.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Let's go ahead and create a table of contents.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>To save some time, I'll paste in a set of links that is my table of contents.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And as you can see, these are all local links to content on the page which is recognizable with this hash (#) symbol before these ids.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, the articles themselves are actually where we would place ids so this one would be called 'id=soup', and then we would have set the id for the salad recipe, and we will set the id for the pizza recipe.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now, we have the very top of the page, a little table of contents and if I click, I'll be brought down to each of these recipes.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>Now that's what we want, it looks great.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>I think that's a great step forward.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>But again, if I was developing this page and imagine we had 20 recipes on this page.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And I come to this as a developer, may not immediately understand the purpose of this set of links.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And if I'm a screen reader, I, too, might don't know what this group of links is for so this is where the 'nav' semantic element comes in.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>By surrounding this list of links with the 'nav' semantic tag, we're sharing more information about the intent or the meaning of the set of links.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>We're telling the screen readers, we're telling the developers that this is meant as a navigation element for our page, and perhaps in certain browsers, these navigation links may show up differently and allow us to visualize this set of links in a different manner.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>So that's it. Now we have our page, I'll just save it.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>You can see that it's a richer page from when we started and it has some of the main elements that I wanted to show you as well as some semantic tags.</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p>And that concludes this live coding session. Bon appétit !</p>
			</div>
			<div>
				<p> </p>
			</div></div></body>
</html>
